So GT consists of exactly these term types (and nothing else):
- an \(x^3\) term
- an \(x\) term and a \(t x\) term (both linear in \(x\), at most linear in \(t\))
- a pure \(\sin(v)\) term (no scaling inside sine except 1, no phase shift needed but allowed if it can be set to match)
- **no** \(v\), \(v^3\), \(v^5\), \(\exp(\cdot)\), \(\log(\cdot)\), \(\cos(\cdot)\), \(|v|\), \(v/\sqrt{c+v^2}\), constants, etc.
